Dear Hussein 

 

Hope you are fine, it's just a reminder about your tasks in Expat Legal Portal

1-      Please finish the other forms, make sure that add and update with upload file is working.

2-      Try to find the action of "close button" - not important; if you didn't find it-Don't waste time.

3-      Create "case summary" sheet in PDF format.

*This sheet will display all the data related to that case, sample of the design is attached

*This sheet will be downloaded from the homepage. Near each case ID , create a small button to download this sheet.

      4-     Create on Java class called "Query Class" and move all the SQL queries within the code to that class. Sample is attached

 

Thanks 

Mohammed Abbas
